                     oldWidth = window.innerWidth;
 
                 EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener = function (eventName, eventHandler, useCapture) {
                     if (eventName === "resize") {
                         originalAddEventListener.call(this, eventName, function (event) {
                             if (oldWidth === window.innerWidth) {
                                 return;
                             }
                             else if (oldWidth !== window.innerWidth) {
                                 oldWidth = window.innerWidth;
                             }
                             if (eventHandler.handleEvent) {
                                 eventHandler.handleEvent.call(this, event);
                             }
                             else {
                                 eventHandler.call(this, event);
                             };
                         }, useCapture);
                     }
                     else {
                         originalAddEventListener.call(this, eventName, eventHandler, useCapture);
                     };
                 };
             };

                <a href="https://www.osko-it.de/shopware-beratung/">
                 Shopware
                </a>
                -Projektes und der leistungsstarken
                <a href="https://www.osko-it.de/vario-warenwirtschaft/">
                 VARIO 8 Warenwirtschaft
                </a>
                erreichen Sie genau das, worauf es ankommt: SALES!
                <br/>
                Wir beraten Sie entsprechend Ihren Vorgaben und Wünschen, da wir durch unsere
                <em>
                 Shopware-Zertifizierung
                </em>
                sowie die Realisierung zahlreicher Online-Shops genau wissen, wie der
                <em>
                 E-Commerce
                </em>
                Markt tickt und wohin er sich entwickelt.
               </p>
              </div>

   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 
             jQuery('#wpcs_tab_4535').click(function($){
 
                 if( ! (jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').hasClass('is_open')) ){
 
                     // Open slider
                     wpcs_open_slider_4535();
 
                 } else {
 
                     // close slider
                     wpcs_close_slider_4535();
 
                 }
 
             });
 
             jQuery("#wpcs_overlay_4535, #wpcs_close_slider_4535").click(function(){
                 wpcs_close_slider_4535();
             });
 
             
         });
 
         function wpcs_open_slider_4535(do_repeat){
 
             do_repeat = typeof do_repeat !== 'undefined' ? do_repeat : 0 ;
 
             if( do_repeat !== 0 ){
                 jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').addClass('do_repeat');
                 jQuery( "#wpcs_content_main_4535" ).data( "interval", do_repeat );
             }
 
             if( ! (jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').hasClass('is_open')) && !(jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').hasClass('is_opening')) ){
 
                 // hide tap
                 jQuery('#wpcs_tab_4535,.wpcs_tab').fadeTo("slow", 0);
 
                 jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').addClass('is_opening');
 
                 jQuery("#wpcs_overlay_4535").addClass('wpcs_overlay_display_cross');
 
                 jQuery( "#wpcs_overlay_4535").fadeIn('fast');
 
                 // PRO FEATURE - PUSH BODY
                 
                 jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').addClass('is_open');
 
                 jQuery( "#wpcs_content_main_4535" ).animate({
                     opacity: 1,
                 right: "+=500"
             }, 250 , function() {
 
                     // hide tap
                     jQuery('#wpcs_tab_4535,.wpcs_tab').fadeTo("slow", 0);
 
                     // Trigger some thing here once completely open
                     jQuery( "#wpcs_content_inner_4535").fadeTo("slow" , 1);
 
                     // Remove is_opening class
                     jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').removeClass('is_opening');
 
                 });
 
             }
 
         }
 
         function wpcs_close_slider_4535(){
 
             if( (jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').hasClass('is_open')) && !(jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').hasClass('is_closing')) ) {
 
                 jQuery("#wpcs_overlay_4535").removeClass('wpcs_overlay_display_cross');
 
                 jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').addClass('is_closing');
 
                 jQuery("#wpcs_content_main_4535").animate({
                 right:
                 "-=500"
             }
             , 250 ,
                 function () {
 
                     // Trigger some thing here once completely close
                     jQuery("#wpcs_content_main_4535").fadeTo("fast", 0);
                     jQuery("#wpcs_content_inner_4535").slideUp('fast');
                     jQuery("#wpcs_overlay_4535").fadeOut('slow');
                     jQuery('body').removeClass('fixed-body');
 
                     //  Removing is_open class in the end to avoid any confliction
                     jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').removeClass('is_open');
                     jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').removeClass('is_closing');
 
 
                     // display tap
                     jQuery('#wpcs_tab_4535,.wpcs_tab').fadeTo("slow", 1);
 
                 });
 
                 if( (jQuery('#wpcs_content_main_4535').hasClass('do_repeat')) ) {
                     setTimeout(function () {
                         wpcs_open_slider_4535(0);
                     }, 0 );
                 }
 
             }
 
         }
   </script>

    function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
 					var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";
 					errorMessage += "<br> This includes make eliminates the revolution slider libraries, and make it not work.";
 					errorMessage += "<br><br> To fix it you can:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. In the Slider Settings -> Troubleshooting set option:  <strong><b>Put JS Includes To Body</b></strong> option to true.";
 					errorMessage += "<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2. Find the double jquery.js include and remove it.";
 					errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
 						jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);
 				}
   </script>
